Menghapus Data yang Kosong#

df.dropna(inplace=True)

Cleaning Data#

import re, string

# Text Cleaning
def cleaning(text):
    # Menghapus tag HTML
    text = re.compile('<.*?>|&([a-z0-9]+|#[0-9]{1,6}|#x[0-9a-f]{1,6});').sub('', str(text))

    # Mengubah seluruh teks menjadi huruf kecil
    text = text.lower()

    # Menghapus spasi pada teks
    text = text.strip()

    # Menghapus Tanda Baca, karakter spesial, and spasi ganda
    text = re.compile('<.*?>').sub('', text)
    text = re.compile('[%s]' % re.escape(string.punctuation)).sub(' ', text)
    text = re.sub('\s+', ' ', text)
    text = re.sub(r'\n', ' ', text)
    text = re.sub("â", "", text)

    # Menghapus Nomor
    text = re.sub(r'\[[0-9]*\]', ' ', text)
    text = re.sub(r'[^\w\s]', '', str(text).lower().strip())
    text = re.sub(r'\d', ' ', text)
    text = re.sub(r'\s+', ' ', text)

    # Mengubah text yang berisi 'nan' dengan whitespace agar nantinya dapat dihapus
    text = re.sub('nan', '', text)

    return text

Implementasi Fungsi Pada Data Frame Abstrak#

df['Abstrak'] = df['Abstrak'].apply(lambda x: cleaning(x))

Stopword Data#

Mengubah isi dokumen sesuai dengan kamus data

Import Library NLTK#

nltk.download('stopwords')

[nltk_data] Downloading package stopwords to /root/nltk_data...
[nltk_data]   Package stopwords is already up-to-date!

True

Implementasi Library pada Data#

from nltk.corpus import stopwords
from itertools import chain

stop_words = set(chain(stopwords.words('indonesian')))
df['abstrak_tokens'] = df['abstrak_tokens'].apply(lambda x: [w for w in x if not w in stop_words])

df['Abstrak'] = df['abstrak_tokens'].apply(lambda tokens: ' '.join(tokens))

df[["Abstrak", "abstrak_tokens"]].head()

Steaming Data#

Mengubah kata menjadi bentuk dasar

Import Library Sastrawi#

!pip install sastrawi

Requirement already satisfied: sastrawi in /usr/local/lib/python3.10/dist-packages (1.0.1)

Implementasi Library pada Data#

from Sastrawi.Stemmer.StemmerFactory import StemmerFactory
from tqdm.auto import tqdm
tqdm.pandas()

factory = StemmerFactory()
stemmer = factory.create_stemmer()

df['abstrak_tokens'] = df['abstrak_tokens'].progress_apply(lambda x: stemmer.stem(' '.join(x)).split(' '))

df['Abstrak'] = df['abstrak_tokens'].apply(lambda tokens: ' '.join(tokens))

from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import CountVectorizer

df_countvect = pd.DataFrame(data = X_count.toarray(),columns = terms_count)

import gensim
from gensim.models import Word2Vec
from gensim.test.utils import common_texts
import pandas as pd

sentences = df['abstrak_tokens'].tolist()

model = Word2Vec(sentences, vector_size=100, window=1, sg=1, epochs=1)

word = "hasil"
similar_words = model.wv.most_similar(word)

print(f"Kata yang mirip dengan '{word}':")
for w, sim in similar_words:
    print(f"{w}: {sim:.4f}")

import gensim
from gensim.models import Word2Vec
import pandas as pd

sentences = df['abstrak_tokens'].tolist()

model = Word2Vec(sentences, vector_size=100, window=1, sg=1, epochs=1)

word = "gerak"
context_words = []

if word in model.wv:
    word_vector = model.wv[word]
    similar_words = model.wv.most_similar([word_vector], topn=3)
    context_words = [w for w, _ in similar_words]

print(f"Kata-kata dalam konteks window=1 untuk '{word}':")
for w in context_words:
    print(w)

Kata-kata dalam konteks window=1 untuk 'gerak':
gerak
bas
main

import gensim
from gensim.models import Word2Vec

model = Word2Vec(sentences, vector_size=100, window=1, sg=1, epochs=1)

word1 = "gerak"
word2 = "genetika"

if word1 in model.wv and word2 in model.wv:
    vector1 = model.wv[word1]
    vector2 = model.wv[word2]
    similarity = model.wv.cosine_similarities(vector1, [vector2])[0]

    print(f"Kesamaan kosakata antara '{word1}' dan '{word2}': {similarity:.4f}")
else:
    print("Salah satu atau kedua kata tidak ada dalam model.")

Kesamaan kosakata antara 'gerak' dan 'genetika': 0.4234

doc_topic_proportions = lda_model.transform(df_countvect)

for i, doc in enumerate(df['Abstrak']):
    print(f"Dokumen {i+1}:")
    for j, topic_prob in enumerate(doc_topic_proportions[i]):
        print(f"Topik {j+1}: {topic_prob:.4f}")
    print()

Topik 3: 0.0011

topic_word_distributions = lda_model.components_
feature_names = vectorizer.get_feature_names_out()

for topic_idx, topic in enumerate(topic_word_distributions):
    top_words_idx = topic.argsort()[::-1]  # Mengurutkan indeks kata berdasarkan distribusi topik
    top_words = [feature_names[i] for i in top_words_idx]
    print(f"Topik {topic_idx + 1}:")
    print(", ".join(top_words))
    print()

topic_word_distributions = lda_model.components_
total_word_counts_per_topic = topic_word_distributions.sum(axis=1)  # Total distribusi kata untuk setiap topik

feature_names = vectorizer.get_feature_names_out()

for topic_idx, topic in enumerate(topic_word_distributions):
    top_words_idx = topic.argsort()[::-1]  # Mengurutkan indeks kata berdasarkan distribusi topik
    total_word_count = total_word_counts_per_topic[topic_idx]

    print(f"Topik {topic_idx + 1}:")
    for word_idx in top_words_idx:
        word = feature_names[word_idx]
        word_weight = topic[word_idx] / total_word_count  # Hitung bobot kata untuk topik ini
        print(f"{word}: {word_weight:.4f}")
    print()

import pandas as pd

# Mengonversi distribusi kata dalam setiap topik menjadi DataFrame
topic_word_distributions = lda_model.components_
feature_names = vectorizer.get_feature_names_out()

# Membuat daftar untuk menyimpan data
data = []

for topic_idx, topic in enumerate(topic_word_distributions):
    top_words_idx = topic.argsort()[::-1]
    top_words = [feature_names[i] for i in top_words_idx]
    top_word_weights = [topic[i] for i in top_words_idx]

    # Menambahkan data ke dalam list
    for word, weight in zip(top_words, top_word_weights):
        data.append([topic_idx + 1, word, weight])

# Membuat DataFrame dari data
df = pd.DataFrame(data, columns=['Topik', 'Kata', 'Bobot'])

# Menampilkan DataFrame sebagai tabel
print(df)

Clustering#

from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.cluster import KMeans
import numpy as np

# Assuming df['abstrak_tokens'] contains your sentences
sentences = df['Kata'].tolist()

# Convert sentences to TF-IDF vectors
tfidf_vectorizer = TfidfVectorizer()
tfidf_matrix = tfidf_vectorizer.fit_transform(sentences)

# Perform K-means clustering
num_clusters = 2  # You can change this to the desired number of clusters
kmeans = KMeans(n_clusters=num_clusters, random_state=0, n_init=10)
kmeans.fit(tfidf_matrix)

# Get cluster labels for each sentence
cluster_labels = kmeans.labels_

# Get cluster centers
cluster_centers = kmeans.cluster_centers_

# Print cluster labels and cluster centers
print("Cluster Labels:")
print(cluster_labels)
print("Cluster Centers:")
print(cluster_centers)
